**Candidate 17:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2 + c3*epsilon**c4*exp(T*c5) + c6*epsilon**c7*exp(T*c8)`
Two exp(T) terms. If c5=0 and c8=0: no T dependence. Can't get linear T from exp. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 18:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*sin(T*c3 + c4) + c5 + c6*epsilon**c7 + c8*epsilon`
sin(T*c3) can't match linear T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 19:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2 + c3*epsilon*(T + c4)**c5 + c6*epsilon**c7*exp(T*c8)`
If c8=0: c6*epsilon^c7. If c5=1: c3*epsilon*(T+c4) = c3*epsilon*T + c3*c4*epsilon. Then: c0*epsilon^c1 + c2 + c3*epsilon*T + c3*c4*epsilon + c6*epsilon^c7. This gives epsilon*T, not epsilon^c*T. GT needs T*epsilon^0.626. **NO MATCH** (unless we can get fractional power, but c3*epsilon*(T+c4)^c5 with c5≠1 gives nonlinear T dependence)

**Candidate 20:** exp(c8/T^(1/3)) can't match linear T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 21:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2 + c3*log(T*c4 + 1) + c5*epsilon**c6 + c7*epsilon`
log(T) can't match linear T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 22:** Has 1/T, can't match. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 23:** No T dependence at all. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 24:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 25:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4*epsilon/(T*c5 + c6) + c7/(T*c5 + c6) + c8`
Rational in T, not linear. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 26-34:** No T dependence. **NO MATCH** for all.

**Candidate 35:** `c0*epsilon + c1 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4*epsilon**c5*exp(T**c6*c7)`
exp(T^c6*c7) can't match linear T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 36:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2 + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5*epsilon*(T + c6)**c7 + c8*epsilon`
If c7=1: c5*epsilon*(T+c6) = c5*epsilon*T + c5*c6*epsilon. Gives epsilon*T, not epsilon^0.626*T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 37:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4 + c5*epsilon*(T + c6)**c7`
Same issue - epsilon*(T+c6)^c7. If c7=1: epsilon*T term. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 38:** exp(T*c6) can't match. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 39-40:** No T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 41:** `T*c0/(T*c1 + c2) + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5 + c6*epsilon**c7 + c8/(T*c1 + c2) + c9*epsilon`
T/(T*c1+c2) is rational in T. If c1=0: T*c0/c2 + c8/c2 + rest. Then T*(c0/c2) + c3*epsilon^c4 + c5 + c6*epsilon^c7 + c8/c2 + c9*epsilon. Has T but no T*epsilon^c. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 42-44:** exp terms, no linear T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 43:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4 + c5*epsilon**c6*exp(T*c7)`
exp(T*c7) ≠ linear T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 44:** Same issue. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 45:** `T*c0*log(c1*exp(c2*Abs(epsilon)) + 1) + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5 + c6*epsilon**c7 + c8*epsilon`
T*log(c1*exp(c2*|epsilon|)+1). This is T times a softplus-like function of epsilon. Not T*epsilon^c. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 46:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4 + c5*epsilon**c6 + c7*epsilon`
No T dependence. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 47:** `c0 + c1*epsilon**c2 + c3*epsilon + c4*exp(c5/(T + c6))*Abs(epsilon)**c7`
exp(c5/(T+c6)) can't match linear T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 48:** No T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 49:** `T*c0*log(c1*Abs(epsilon) + 1) + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4 + c5*epsilon**c6 + c7*epsilon`
T*log(c1*|epsilon|+1) ≠ T*epsilon^c. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2 + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5*epsilon + c6*log(T*c7 + 1)*log(c8*Abs(epsilon) + 1)`
log(T)*log(epsilon) ≠ T*epsilon^c. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 51:** `c0*epsilon**c1 + c2 + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5*epsilon + c6*epsilon*exp(T*c7)`
epsilon*exp(T*c7) can't match T*epsilon^0.626. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 52:** `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + T*c2/(c3*epsilon + c4) + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*epsilon**c1 + c8/(c3*epsilon + c4)`
If c3=0: T*c0*epsilon^c1 + T*c2/c4 + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*epsilon^c1 + c8/c4
= T*c0*epsilon^c1 + T*(c2/c4) + c7*epsilon^c1 + c5*epsilon + (c6+c8/c4)
This has T*epsilon^c1, T, epsilon^c1, epsilon, constant. Set c5=0 to remove epsilon. Then: T*epsilon^c1, T, epsilon^c1, constant. **MATCH!**

Verify: c1=0.626, c0=1.518, c2/c4=-0.545, c7=-534.58, c6+c8/c4=191.92. With c3=0, c4=any nonzero, c2=-0.545*c4, c8=(191.92-c6)*c4. Solvable. **MATCH**

**Candidate 53:** exp(c7/(T+c8)) can't match. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 54:** No T dependence (sin of epsilon). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 55-56:** No T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 57:** exp(T*c7) can't match. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 58:** exp(T*c5)*sin(...) + 1/T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 59:** exp(T*c3) can't match. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 60:** cos(T*c7) can't match linear T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 61:** `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*epsilon + c3 + c4*epsilon**c1 + c5*epsilon**c6*exp(T**c7*c8)`
If c8=0: exp(0)=1, so c5*epsilon^c6. Then: T*c0*epsilon^c1 + c2*epsilon + c3 + c4*epsilon^c1 + c5*epsilon^c6. No standalone T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 62:** No T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 63:** exp(T*c7) can't match. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 64:** `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + c2*epsilon + c3 + c4*epsilon**c1 + c5*log(c6*exp(T*c7 + c8*epsilon) + 1)`
The log term is a softplus. Can't exactly match linear T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 65:** `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + T*c2*log(c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + 1) + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*epsilon**c1`
T*log(c3*exp(c4*epsilon)+1) is not linear in T times a power of epsilon. Actually it IS linear in T, but the epsilon dependence is log(exp(epsilon)) which is not epsilon^c. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 66:** `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + T*c2*(c3 + epsilon)**c4 + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*epsilon**c1`
If c3=0: T*c0*epsilon^c1 + T*c2*epsilon^c4 + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*epsilon^c1
For GT: need T*epsilon^0.626 and T (standalone). T standalone requires epsilon^c4 = 1, so c4=0: T*c2. Then: T*c0*epsilon^c1 + T*c2 + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*epsilon^c1. Set c5=0: T*epsilon^c1, T, epsilon^c1, constant. **MATCH!**

With c3=0, c4=0: c1=0.626, c0=1.518, c2=-0.545, c7=-534.58, c6=191.92, c5=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 67:** `T*c0/(T*c1+c2) + T*c3*epsilon**c4/(T*c1+c2) + c5/(T*c1+c2) + c6*epsilon**c4/(T*c1+c2) + c7*epsilon/(T*c1+c2) + c8/(T*c1+c2)`
Factor out 1/(T*c1+c2): [T*c0 + T*c3*epsilon^c4 + c5 + c6*epsilon^c4 + c7*epsilon + c8]/(T*c1+c2)
If c1=0: [T*c0 + T*c3*epsilon^c4 + (c5+c8) + c6*epsilon^c4 + c7*epsilon]/c2
= T*(c0+c3*epsilon^c4)/c2 + [(c5+c8) + c6*epsilon^c4 + c7*epsilon]/c2
This gives T, T*epsilon^c4, epsilon^c4, epsilon, constant. Set c7=0: T, T*epsilon^c4, epsilon^c4, constant. **MATCH!**

**Candidate 68:** Similar rational form. If c1=0: everything divided by c2. Numerator: T*c0 + T*c3 + T*c4*epsilon^c5 + T*c6*epsilon + c7 + c8*epsilon^c5 + c9*epsilon. Divided by c2: T*(c0+c3)/c2 + T*c4*epsilon^c5/c2 + T*c6*epsilon/c2 + c7/c2 + c8*epsilon^c5/c2 + c9*epsilon/c2. Has T*epsilon term which GT doesn't need. Set c6=0: T*(c0+c3)/c2 + T*c4*epsilon^c5/c2 + c7/c2 + c8*epsilon^c5/c2 + c9*epsilon/c2. Set c9=0: T, T*epsilon^c5, epsilon^c5, constant. **MATCH!**

**Candidate 69:** `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**c2 + c3*epsilon**c2 + c4*epsilon + c5`
Terms: T, T*epsilon^c2, epsilon^c2, epsilon, constant. Set c4=0: T, T*epsilon^c2, epsilon^c2, constant. **MATCH!**

**Candidate 70:** `T*c0 + T*c1 + T*c2*epsilon**c3 + c4 + c5*epsilon**c3 + c6*epsilon`
= T*(c0+c1) + T*c2*epsilon^c3 + c4 + c5*epsilon^c3 + c6*epsilon. Set c6=0: T, T*epsilon^c3, epsilon^c3, constant. **MATCH!**

**Candidate 71:** `T*c0*epsilon**c1 + T*c2/(T*c3 + c4) + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7/(T*c3 + c4) + c8*epsilon**c1`
If c3=0: T*c0*epsilon^c1 + T*c2/c4 + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7/c4 + c8*epsilon^c1
= T*c0*epsilon^c1 + T*(c2/c4) + c5*epsilon + (c6+c7/c4) + c8*epsilon^c1. Set c5=0: **MATCH!**

**Candidate 72:** If c1=0: numerator/c2. Numerator: T*c0+T*c3+T*c4*epsilon^c5+T*c6*epsilon^c5+c7+c8*epsilon^c5+c9*epsilon^c5. = T*(c0+c3) + T*(c4+c6)*epsilon^c5 + c7 + (c8+c9)*epsilon^c5. Divided by c2: T, T*epsilon^c5, constant, epsilon^c5. **MATCH!**

**Candidate 73:** If c1=0: [T*c0+T*c3+T*c4*epsilon^c5+c6+c7*epsilon^c5+c8]/c2 = T*(c0+c3)/c2 + T*c4*epsilon^c5/c2 + (c6+c8)/c2 + c7*epsilon^c5/c2. = T, T*epsilon^c5, constant, epsilon^c5. **MATCH!**

**Candidate 74:** `T*c0 + T*c1 + T*c2*epsilon**c3 + T*c4*epsilon**c3 + c5 + c6*epsilon**c3 + c7*epsilon**c3`
= T*(c0+c1) + T*(c2+c4)*epsilon^c3 + c5 + (c6+c7)*epsilon^c3. = T, T*epsilon^c3, constant, epsilon^c3. **MATCH!**

**Candidate 75:** `T*c0 + T*c1 + T*c2*epsilon**c3 + c4*epsilon**c3 + c5`
= T*(c0+c1) + T*c2*epsilon^c3 + c4*epsilon^c3 + c5. = T, T*epsilon^c3, epsilon^c3, constant. **MATCH!**
